* [`NullRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/nullrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with (possibly) null values. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/NullRules)._
* [`OptionalRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/optionalrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `Optional`s. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/OptionalRules)._
* [`PatternRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/patternrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to code dealing with regular expressions. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/PatternRules)._
* [`PreconditionsRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/preconditionsrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster templates related to statements dealing with `Preconditions`. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/PreconditionsRules)._
* [`PrimitiveRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/primitiverulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with primitives. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/PrimitiveRules)._
* [`RandomGeneratorRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/randomgeneratorrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `RandomGenerator` instances. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/RandomGeneratorRules)._
* [`RxJava2AdapterRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/rxjava2adapterrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `RxJava2Adapter`. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/RxJava2AdapterRules)._
* [`StreamRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/streamrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `Stream`s. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/StreamRules)._
* [`StringRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/stringrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `String`s. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/StringRules)._
* [`SuggestedFixRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/suggestedfixrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `SuggestedFix`es. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/SuggestedFixRules)._
* [`TimeRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/timerulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with time. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/TimeRules)._
* [`WebClientRules` Refaster recipes](/recipes/tech/picnic/errorprone/refasterrules/webclientrulesrecipes.md) - _Refaster rules related to expressions dealing with `org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient` and related types. [Source](https://error-prone.picnic.tech/refasterrules/WebClientRules)._
## rewrite-vulncheck

* [Use VulnCheck Exploit Intelligence to fix vulnerabilities](/recipes/vulncheck/fixvulncheckvulnerabilities.md) - _This software composition analysis (SCA) tool detects and upgrades dependencies with publicly disclosed vulnerabilities. This recipe both generates a report of vulnerable dependencies and upgrades to newer versions with fixes. This recipe by default only upgrades to the latest **patch** version.  If a minor or major upgrade is required to reach the fixed version, this can be controlled using the `maximumUpgradeDelta` option. Vulnerability information comes from VulnCheck Vulnerability Intelligence. The recipe has an option to limit fixes to only those vulnerabilities that have evidence of exploitation at various levels of severity._
## rewrite-xml

* [Add a comment to an XML tag](/recipes/xml/addcommenttoxmltag.md) - _Adds a comment as the first element in an XML tag._
* [Add date bounds to OWASP suppressions](/recipes/xml/security/addowaspdateboundsuppressions.md) - _Adds an expiration date to all OWASP suppressions in order to ensure that they are periodically reviewed. For use with the OWASP `dependency-check` tool. More details: https://jeremylong.github.io/DependencyCheck/general/suppression.html._
* [Add new XML attribute for an Element](/recipes/xml/addtagattribute.md) - _Add new XML attribute with value on a specified element._
* [Blank lines](/recipes/xml/format/linebreaks.md) - _Add line breaks at appropriate places between XML syntax elements._
* [Find OWASP vulnerability suppression XML files](/recipes/xml/security/isowaspsuppressionsfile.md) - _These files are used to suppress false positives in OWASP [Dependency Check](https://jeremylong.github.io/DependencyCheck)._
* [Find XML namespace URIs](/recipes/xml/search/hasnamespaceuri.md) - _Find XML namespace URIs, optionally restricting the search by a XPath expression._
* [Find XML namespace prefixes](/recipes/xml/search/findnamespaceprefix.md) - _Find XML namespace prefixes, optionally restricting the search by a XPath expression._
* [Find XML tags](/recipes/xml/search/findtags.md) - _Find XML tags by XPath expression._
* [Find files without Namespace URI](/recipes/xml/search/doesnotusenamespaceuri.md) - _Find XML root elements that do not have a specific Namespace URI, optionally restricting the search by an XPath expression._
* [Format XML](/recipes/xml/format/autoformat.md) - _Indents XML using the most common indentation size and tabs or space choice in use in the file._
* [Normalize format](/recipes/xml/format/normalizeformat.md) - _Move whitespace to the outermost LST element possible._
* [Normalize line breaks](/recipes/xml/format/normalizelinebreaks.md) - _Consistently use either Windows style (CRLF) or Linux style (LF) line breaks. If no `GeneralFormatStyle` is specified this will use whichever style of line endings are more common._
* [Normalize to tabs or spaces](/recipes/xml/format/normalizetabsorspaces.md) - _Consistently use either tabs or spaces in indentation._
* [Remove empty XML Tag](/recipes/xml/removeemptyxmltags.md) - _Removes XML tags that do not have attributes or children, including self closing tags._
* [Remove out-of-date OWASP suppressions](/recipes/xml/security/removeowaspsuppressions.md) - _Remove all OWASP suppressions with a suppression end date in the past, as these are no longer valid. For use with the OWASP `dependency-check` tool. More details on OWASP suppression files can be found [here](https://jeremylong.github.io/DependencyCheck/general/suppression.html)._
* [Remove trailing whitespace](/recipes/xml/removetrailingwhitespace.md) - _Remove any extra trailing whitespace from the end of each line._
* [Tabs and indents](/recipes/xml/format/tabsandindents.md) - _Format tabs and indents in XML code._
* [Update OWASP suppression date bounds](/recipes/xml/security/updateowaspsuppressiondate.md) - _Updates the expiration date for OWASP suppressions having a matching cve tag. For use with the OWASP `dependency-check` tool. More details: https://jeremylong.github.io/DependencyCheck/general/suppression.html._
* [XML style Auto-detection debug](/recipes/xml/style/autodetectdebug.md) - _Runs XML Autodetect and records the results in data tables and search markers. A debugging tool for figuring out why XML documents get styled the way they do._
* [XSLT transformation](/recipes/xml/xslttransformation.md) - _Apply the specified XSLT transformation on matching files. Note that there are no format matching guarantees when running this recipe._
